 metro kii oparational cost main badhotareeis bichadilli metrone tamaam vajahon kaa hawala diya he, jisase use kiraaya badhanaa pad rahaa he
 According to an officer of Delhi Metro Rail Corporation, the last time Delhi Metro fares were increased in 2009, the operational cost of the metro has increased compared to that, there is no option but to increase the fare of the metro to overcome it
 ye he dilli metro kii daleelmetro kii daleel ke mutabik march 2009 main metro ko bijli 3 rupye 21 paise prati unit milti thi, jo march 2017 main 6 rupee 58 paise ho gai
 This means that the price of electricity received by the metro has increased by 105 percent
 isi tarah metro kii daleel he ki 2009 main uske staff kii cost ek karod 17 lakh rupee prati kilometre thi, jo 2017 main badhkar 2 karod 80 lakh rupee prati kilometre ho gai he yani staff cost main 139 fisadi kii badhotaree hui he
